  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.

### Tarot

- `P.1`
  Frame: The Magician
  Movement: Route through the return gate, then lock the structure, keeping the line aligned with four port convergence produces four distinct finished products from single.
  Reading: fluid conduit / structural fixation / return gate line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P.10`
  Frame: The High Priestess
  Movement: Circulate the charge, then clamp and test the flow, then let the fraction settle, keeping the line aligned with four port convergence produces four distinct finished products from single.
  Reading: commit checkpoint / valve clamp / circulation command line.
  Confidence: strong

  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A full convergence page: oscillate work↔settle until the volatile/solute balance locks, then expose four named output ports as the reusable "finished states." Process statistics: 85 circulation commands (qo-); 13 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 16 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 4 completion markers (daiin); 2 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f83v` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=85, N_valve=13, and N_seal=2. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f83v` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A full convergence page: oscillate work↔settle until the volatile/solute balance locks, then expose four named output ports as the reusable "finished states."`

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f83v} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]

\[

The formal theorem of `f83v` is:

1. the page is a purification controller, not an ornamental bath,
2. circulation and clamp logic dominate the visible route,
3. the stable state is published only after salt/commit evidence is satisfied,
4. the folio's distinctive role is `Four-port distribution`.
